        // Simple button interaction
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const buttons = document.querySelectorAll('.btn-primary, .btn-secondary');
            
            buttons.forEach(button => {
                button.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                    e.preventDefault();
                    
                    // Add click animation
                    this.style.transform = 'scale(0.98)';
                    
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        this.style.transform = '';
                    }, 150);
                    
                    // For demo purposes - show alert
                    const buttonText = this.textContent.trim();
                    alert(`You clicked: ${buttonText}\nThis would navigate to the appropriate page.`);
                });
                
                // Touch device support
                button.addEventListener('touchstart', function() {
                    this.classList.add('active');
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        this.classList.remove('active');
                    }, 300);
                });
            });
            
            // Add CSS for active state
            const style = document.createElement('style');
            style.textContent = `
                .btn-primary.active, .btn-secondary.active {
                    transform: scale(0.98) !important;
                }
            `;
            document.head.appendChild(style);
        });

    <script>
        // Number counting animation
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function() {
            const statNumbers = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-number');
            
            statNumbers.forEach(number => {
                const originalText = number.textContent;
                
                // Check if it contains a plus sign
                if (originalText.includes('+')) {
                    const numValue = parseInt(originalText);
                    if (!isNaN(numValue)) {
                        // Reset for animation
                        number.textContent = '0+';
                        
                        let counter = 0;
                        const increment = numValue / 25; // Smooth animation
                        
                        const timer = setInterval(() => {
                            counter += increment;
                            if (counter >= numValue) {
                                number.textContent = originalText;
                                clearInterval(timer);
                            } else {
                                number.textContent = Math.floor(counter) + '+';
                            }
                        }, 50);
                    }
                }
            });
            
            // Add hover effects
            const statCards = document.querySelectorAll('.stat-card');
            statCards.forEach(card => {
                card.addEventListener('mouseenter', function() {
                    this.style.transform = 'translateY(-10px)';
                    this.style.boxShadow = '0 25px 50px rgba(230, 41, 104, 0.15)';
                });
                
                card.addEventListener('mouseleave', function() {
                    this.style.transform = 'translateY(0)';
                    this.style.boxShadow = '0 15px 35px rgba(0, 0, 0, 0.05)';
                });
                
                // Touch device support
                card.addEventListener('touchstart', function() {
                    this.classList.add('hover-effect');
                    setTimeout(() => {
                        this.classList.remove('hover-effect');
                    }, 300);
                });
            });
            
            // Add CSS for touch effect
            const style = document.createElement('style');
            style.textContent = `
                .stat-card.hover-effect {
                    transform: translateY(-10px) !important;
                    box-shadow: 0 25px 50px rgba(230, 41, 104, 0.15) !important;
                    border-color: #E62968 !important;
                }
                
                .stat-card.hover-effect .stat-icon {
                    background: linear-gradient(135deg, #E62968, #ff6b9d) !important;
                    color: white !important;
                    transform: scale(1.1) !important;
                }
                
                .stat-card.hover-effect .stat-number {
                    color: #E62968 !important;
                }
                
                .stat-card.hover-effect .stat-tag {
                    background: #E62968 !important;
                    color: white !important;
                    transform: translateY(-2px) !important;
                }
            `;
            document.head.appendChild(style);
        });
    </script>

			objCarousel.owlCarousel({
                loop: true,      
                navText: ["<i class='fas fa-arrow-left'></i>","<i class='fas fa-arrow-right'></i>"],
                nav: true,
                rtl:false,
				dots: true,
                center: false,
                paddingType: "none",
                autoplay: false,
                autoplayTimeout: 5000,
                autoplayHoverPause: true,
                smartSpeed: 1000,

					768 : {
						items:2,
                                    
                        	            
					},
					980 : {
						items:3,
                                    
                        	            
					}
				}
			});

      	objCarousel.trigger("replace.owl.carousel",htmlItems);
      	objCarousel.trigger("refresh.owl.carousel");
         
    });
